<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нуться</a> (7315)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуть.html>сдви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdvínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвигаться.html>сдвига́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move, to budge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нулся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>sdvínulsja</b> s mésta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he never budged</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come/draw together</li>
<li>to move forward, to get going, to improve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чки</a>) (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ле</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:требующий.html>тре́бующем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ний</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:действие.html>де́йствий</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdvínutʹsja</b> s mésta (mjórtvoj tóčki) (o déle, trébujuščem rešénij, déjstvij)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin to move forward (get going; improve)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нулся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">voprós ne <b>sdvínulsja</b> s mésta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">no headway has been made in the matter</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуться.html>сдви́нулось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délo <b>sdvínulosʹ</b> s mésta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">things began to move</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдвинуть.html>сдви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>сдви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделавшийся.html>сделавшийся</a> (1989)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́латься</a>.

***сделать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сделать</a> (130)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">délatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdélatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make, to do
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:замечание.html>замеча́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdélatʹ</b> zamečánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pass a remark, to make a remark</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сде́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лать</b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">сдѣлать</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-де-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-л-а</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>.  | Кузнецова, Ефремова, 1986 |

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделаться.html>сде́латься</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdélatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́латься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become, to get, to grow, to turn</li>
<li>to happen (with, to), to be going on</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdélatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>сде́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лать<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:делаться.html>де́латься</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-дел-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdélka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сделка.html>сде́лок</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержанность.html>сде́ржанность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdéržannostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержанность.html>сде́ржанности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержанность.html>сде́ржанности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержанность.html>сде́ржанностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>restraint, self-restraint
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержанность.html>сде́ржанность</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">projavljátʹ <b>sdéržannostʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">show <b>restraint</b></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>reserve, moderateness</li></ol>

Зализняка).

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сде́ржанный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdéržannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>restrained, reserved <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">held back, limited, kept in check or under control</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-держ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства_2"></span></h3>

<p><b>сде́р<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жан<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-держ-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
</p>

***сдержать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сдержа́ть</a> (6588)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">deržátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сдержа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sderžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>держа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдерживать.html>сде́рживать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hold in, to hold back, to keep back, to restrain, to hold in check, to contain, to deter</li>
<li>to keep (promise, word)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержать.html>сде́ржанный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sdéržannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to control/restrain oneself, to hold oneself in check
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдержаться.html>сдержа́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on jedvá <b>sderžálsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he could hardly contain himself</span></div></dd>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:содрать.html>содра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strip, to strip off, to scratch off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdirátʹ</b> kóžu (s)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to skin; strip the skin off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кору́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> берёзы</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdirátʹ</b> korú s berjózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bark a birch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шкура.html>шку́ру</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тного</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdirátʹ</b> škúru s živótnovo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to flay/skin an animal</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сдирать.html>сдира́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:бешеный.html>бе́шеную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>це́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sdirátʹ</b> s kovó-libo béšenuju cénu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rip someone off; charge someone an exorbitant price</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to copy, to crib, to plagiarize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдохнуть.html>сдо́хнуть</a> (7112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóxnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдохнуть.html>сдо́хнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sdóxnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сдыха́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>до́хнуть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to die <i>(of livestock, cattle; battery)</i></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдуть.html>сдуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sdutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдувать.html>сдува́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sduvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сдуть.html>сдуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сду́нуть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow away, to blow off

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сдуть.html>сду́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak vétrom sdúlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">gone [he disappeared] in a split second</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crib <i>(from)</i></li></ol>

***себя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> (40)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sebe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swé</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sebjá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(reflexive pronoun)</i> myself, yourself, himself, herself, itself, ourselves, yourselves, themselves (no nominative case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ljúbit <b>sebjá</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He loves himself.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ljubljú <b>sebjá</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I love myself.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú ne po sebé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He feels out of sorts.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мне</a> ка́к-то <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne kák-to ne po sebé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t feel quite myself.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувствовать.html>чу́вствует</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></b> лу́чше.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná čúvstvujet <b>sebjá</b> lúčše.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She’s feeling better.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní u <b>sebjá</b> v kómnate.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They're in their room.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаемый.html>зна́ем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My znájem <b>sebjá</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We know ourselves.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себе́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja pojédu k sebé.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I will to go to my place.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(reflexive pronoun)</i> oneself</li></ol>
